```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([AlertMeToggle Component Render]) --> CheckProps[Check Props]
    CheckProps --> GetState[Get Redux State via useSelector]
    GetState --> CheckOrg{Check Active Organization}
    CheckOrg -->|Not Carrier/Shipper| ReturnNull[Return null]
    CheckOrg -->|Is Carrier/Shipper| RenderComponent[Render Component]
    RenderComponent --> RenderTooltip[Render Tooltip with Checkbox]
    RenderComponent --> RenderModal[Render AlertMeModal]
    RenderTooltip --> UserClick{User Clicks Checkbox}
    UserClick --> OnChange[onChange Handler]
    OnChange --> DispatchFetch[Dispatch fetchSubscription]
    DispatchFetch --> CallOnOpen[Call onOpen]
    CallOnOpen --> ShowModal[Set showAlertMeModal = true]
    ShowModal --> ModalOpen[Modal Opens]
    ModalOpen --> UserInteracts{User Interacts}
    UserInteracts -->|Subscribe| DispatchSubscribe[Dispatch subscribe]
    UserInteracts -->|Update| DispatchUpdate[Dispatch updateSubscription]
    UserInteracts -->|Unsubscribe| DispatchUnsubscribe[Dispatch unsubscribe]
    UserInteracts -->|Close| CallOnHide[Call onHide]
    CallOnHide --> HideModal[Set showAlertMeModal = false]
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class AlertMeToggle {
        +checked: bool
        +subscribeeDetails: object
        +displayedId: string
        +subscriptionState: object
        +onModalOpen: func
        +onModalHide: func
        -showAlertMeModal: state
        -dispatch: func
        -t: func
        +onOpen()
        +onHide()
        +onChange(e)
        +render()
    }
    class Checkbox {
        +checked: bool
        +onChange: func
        +icon: object
        +checkedIcon: object
        +iconSize: number
        +color: string
        +checkedColor: string
    }
    class Tooltip {
        +placement: string
        +tooltipChildren: element
        +showDelayInMs: number
    }
    class AlertMeModal {
        +show: bool
        +hide: func
        +subscribeeDetails: object
        +displayedId: string
        +isSubscriptionLoading: bool
        +subscriptionDetails: object
        +subscriptionRequestError: object
        +subscribe: func
        +updateSubscription: func
        +unsubscribe: func
        +isSubscriptionUpdating: bool
        +subscriptionUpdateSuccess: bool
        +subscriptionUpdateError: object
    }
    class SubscriptionState {
        +actionCreators: object
        +selectors: object
    }
    AlertMeToggle --> Checkbox
    AlertMeToggle --> Tooltip
    AlertMeToggle --> AlertMeModal
    AlertMeToggle --> SubscriptionState
    Tooltip --> Checkbox
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant AlertMeToggle
    participant Redux
    participant SubscriptionState
    participant AlertMeModal
    User->>AlertMeToggle: Clicks Checkbox
    AlertMeToggle->>Redux: dispatch(fetchSubscription)
    Redux->>SubscriptionState: actionCreators.fetchSubscription
    AlertMeToggle->>AlertMeToggle: onOpen()
    AlertMeToggle->>AlertMeModal: show = true
    AlertMeModal->>User: Display Modal
    User->>AlertMeModal: Subscribe/Update/Unsubscribe
    AlertMeModal->>Redux: dispatch(action)
    Redux->>SubscriptionState: execute action
    SubscriptionState->>Redux: update state
    Redux->>AlertMeModal: new state
    User->>AlertMeModal: Close Modal
    AlertMeModal->>AlertMeToggle: hide()
    AlertMeToggle->>AlertMeToggle: setShowAlertMeModal(false)
```

stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialized
    Initialized --> CheckingPermissions: Component Mounts
    CheckingPermissions --> Disabled: Not Carrier/Shipper
    CheckingPermissions --> Enabled: Is Carrier/Shipper
    Disabled --> [*]
    Enabled --> Unchecked: checked = false
    Enabled --> Checked: checked = true
    Unchecked --> Loading: User clicks checkbox
    Checked --> Loading: User clicks checkbox
    Loading --> ModalOpen: Fetch subscription
    ModalOpen --> Subscribing: User subscribes
    ModalOpen --> Updating: User updates
    ModalOpen --> Unsubscribing: User unsubscribes
    ModalOpen --> Enabled: User closes modal
    Subscribing --> Success: Operation succeeds
    Subscribing --> Error: Operation fails
    Updating --> Success: Operation succeeds
    Updating --> Error: Operation fails
    Unsubscribing --> Success: Operation succeeds
    Unsubscribing --> Error: Operation fails
    Success --> ModalOpen
    Error --> ModalOpen
